19. [Most Frequently Asked Questions About  Email Marketing](https://techncruncher.blogspot.com/2022/01/most-frequently-asked-questions-about.html)  
<p></p><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgD5ya1-4Tnsum7tKBC7maSYhkX2x5tHg2-_ihpar1PmlsT7MKPH0419APpBlmOXCVkxaozFrSnC23BdOQy6AnChsLoBEDG2qt34GukCtnGjPXwGHpa9AicdbP0EjCMyxbTGYGUPz24NvoC6Ph3zCxOJ1ZhqxeAua4kx-SzwkbngPsWo9dciHSozTstJA=s1920" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span><div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span><a name="more"></a></span>1. Why is email marketing important?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Email is the marketing tool that helps you&nbsp; create a seamless, connected, frictionless buyer journey. More importantly, email marketing allows you to build relationships with prospects, customers, and past customers. It's your chance to speak&nbsp; to them right in their inbox, at a time that suits them. Along with the right message, email can become one of your most powerful marketing channels.</span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">2. What is benefits of email marketing?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Email marketing is best way for creating long term relationship with your clients, and increasing sales in our company.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Benefits of email marketing for bussiness:</span></div><div><ul style="text-align: left;"><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Better brand recognition</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Statistics of what works best</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">More sales</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Targeted audience</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">More traffic to your products/services/newsletter</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Build credibility</span></li></ul></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Most&nbsp; bussinesses are using email marketing and making tons of money with email marketing.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">3. What is the simplest day and time to send my marketing emails?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Again, the answer to this question varies from company to company. And again, testing is the way to find out what works best. Typically, weekends and mornings seem to be&nbsp; times when multiple emails are opened, but since your audience may have different habits, it's best to experiment and then use your&nbsp; data to decide.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">&nbsp;4. Which metrics should I be looking at?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">The two most important metrics for email marketing are&nbsp; open rate and click-through rate. If your emails aren't opened, subscribers will never see your full marketing message, and if they open them but don't click through to your site, your emails won't convert.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">5. How do I write a decent subject line?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">The best subject lines are short and to the point, accurately describing&nbsp; the content of the email, but also catchy and intriguing, so the reader wants to know more. Once Again, this is the perfect place for&nbsp; A/B testing, to see what types of subject lines work best with your audience. Your call to action should be clear and&nbsp; simple. It should be somewhere at the top of your email for those who haven't finished reading the entire email,&nbsp; then repeated&nbsp; at the end for those reading all the way through. It should state exactly what you want subscribers to do, for example "Click here to download the premium theme for free.</span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /><br />

<br />6. Is email marketing still effective?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Email marketing is one of the most effective ways for a business to reach its customers directly. Think about it. You don't post something on your site&nbsp; hoping people will visit it. You don't even post something on a social media page and hope fans&nbsp; see it. You're sending something straight to each person's inbox, where they'll definitely&nbsp; see it! Even if they don't open it, they'll still see your subject line and business name every time you send an email, so you're still communicating directly with your audience.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span><br /></span><br />

<br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">7. However do I grow my email subscribers list? Should i buy an email list or build it myself?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Buying an email list is&nbsp; waste of time &amp; money. These email accounts are unverified and not interested in your brand. The mailing list is useless if your subscribers do not open your emails. There are different ways to grow your mailing list.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span>Give them a free ebook and host it on a landing page where they have to enter the email to download the file and also create a forum page on your website, asks your visitors what questions they might have about your business, and collects email addresses to follow up with them.</span><br />

<br /></span></div>

  <div id="atContainer-05a47ba863f62ec113e14b51b976d14a"></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">8. How do I prevent audience from unsubscribing?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">If the&nbsp; subject line of the email is irrelevant to&nbsp; customers, they will ignore it multiple times. But, if it keeps repeating, they are intercepted and unsubscribed from your emails. So, send relevant emails for the benefit of the customer. Don't send emails that often only focus&nbsp; on sales, offers and discounts.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Submit information about your business and offers so you can connect with customers. You can also update them on recent trends in your industry. The basic role of an email is first and foremost to&nbsp; connect with customers, get the most out of this tool.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">9. What is the difference between a cold email and a spam email?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Cold emails are mostly sales emails that are sent with content align to the needs of the recipient. It is usually personalized and includes a business perspective. However, it is still an unsolicited email. And all unsolicited emails are marked as SPAM.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Regularly receiving this type of unsolicited email in your users' inboxes, chances are&nbsp; your emails will soon be diverted to&nbsp; spam or junk folders. The most important thing to prevent this from happening is to respect your recipients' choice to opt-out of receiving emails from you. You can add the links to easily unsubscribe. You must be familiar with the CAN-SPAM Act and its regulations.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">10. Where can I find email template?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Almost all email campaign tools provide you with ready-made templates. Whether you use MailChimp or Pardot, you'll get several email templates ready to use.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">&nbsp;However, if you want to create a template from scratch, you can do so.Most of email campaign tools have option to paste the HTML code of your own design.&nbsp;</span></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br />11. What email marketing trend will help marketers succeed in 2022?</span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Is it a trend to listen to&nbsp; and get to know your customers? I think people realize how bad it feels for a brand or a company to obsess over themselves without knowing their customers personal needs. People who listen empathetically and then provide value based on what they learn will win.</span></div></div><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span><br /></span><span>Final Saying</span></span></h3><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">&nbsp;You can approach email marketing in different ways. We have compiled a list of most frequently asked questions to help you understand how to get started, what constraints you need to keep in mind, and what future development you will need, we don’t have 100% answers to every situation and there’s always a chance you will have something new and different to deal with as you market your own business.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><br /></div>

20. [7 Free Websites Every Content Creator Needs to Know](https://techncruncher.blogspot.com/2022/01/7-free-websites-every-content-creator.html)  
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjwH3GmjDmHcu86RboQutNZeTWtfl93FX1CXyb3v9r45OyLZAAwlhaOy0qm5SrXo8QN5MuzUWOQqJ5QZg-4aVQOdMGG4HZkQ65y_kyrOUqZhhVMMWlqYUG7MrCIMp4hGVK79ILv7nU7EYAGcyE_HTap6A74fr9L9ui86KozuV2G6niNgmGyEWgf3O2Aag=s1366" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></div><b><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span><a name="more"></a></span>Do you have the desire to become a content creator, but not have the money to start? Here are 7 free websites every content creator needs to know.</span></b><p></p><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">1.Exploding Topics (Trending Topics)</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhNzJJ96Kzlld-aqoaqvMFnBOdDbQ-1CspYnUvKKGHIsbmqt5aZpgowp3SsxV8Od_xs2iL3ygNfuRQlchGRE2vmIEAFMDjQ2lF-He48S8ZzFQPVtITAul06thnaYe1wJapgOpBDKBiGlQ9A54K6vNkl-ln16Ky5kKzraB9yvYntYfF5-WH4bIQpW0W6Kg=s1200" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit:- Exploding Topics)<span><!--more--></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">If you're a content creator, you might be wondering what better way to find new topic ideas than to see what people are searching for? This tool gives you this data without anyone else's explanation. It provides related hashtags and tips on how to use them effectively in your posts. It's a great tool for anyone who wants to keep up to date with what's most relevant in their niche. You can also see the most popular hashtags by country, making it easier to understand cross-border and demographic trends. This site makes your search for content easier than ever! There are countless ways to use explosive topics to your advantage as a content creator.&nbsp;</span></div><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Some examples can be:</span></p><p></p><ul style="text-align: left;"><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Use the most popular hashtags and keywords to get inspiration for ideas.</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">&nbsp;Find out what people are talking about in real-time.</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">&nbsp;Find new audiences you may not have known were interested in your topic.</span></li></ul><p></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">There’s no excuse not to try this website — it’s free and easy to use!</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><a href="https://explodingtopics.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Visit Exploding Topics From Here</a></span></p><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">2. Headline Studio (Headline Grader)</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEg_BImtXlDG4mY8E1M-s7N9jOu5mCNj4xpeck4f4BjnbBk28ufqx8PrbIGztTVFEjJyPgGYSb1c5Lot3i2FFvoTf9hceIdMZ0q0UlzHwIAgekKDQzenRCFDXjjmCDRGVWcweACwx4TWJNkTkLP3qY4MVhAhzHV_NvX827iVC4Isi_5PY1APma3Q86sKqg=s660" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit:-Headline Studio)</span></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><p><span><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span>Headline Studio allows you to create catchy headlines for your content.&nbsp;</span><span>After writing a title there is data on how often people view articles with similar titles and why they are involved with them.</span></span><p></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">This is a valuable tool when creating new blog posts because it generates catchy headlines for your blog post to catch a reader’s attention.</span></p><p><a href="https://coschedule.com/headline-studio" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Visit Headline Studio From Here</span></a></p><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">3. Answer the public</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhDhwDpmPqs-AfaJNuQH-ZI-fg5MSl8TFMFUQLd0-yFurLMLy_1v49EHto_y9A4sI-vfmW5vmIiGnBC2-LKgXOZDXthDwXBGCrRUkwpEHLI42IjYf7tO35yZH4Ru2EUnAeE_FNLbKeqsUEsFFElGZ1ZfxVH5SyD0VFFstvvN8xUms5oG55piVEgGQ7Zgw=s665" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit:- Answer The Public)</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><p><span><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Answer The public is an excellent tool for content creators. It gives you insight into what people are asking on social media sites and communities and lets you guess about topics that matter to your audience. Answer the public allows you to enter a keyword or topic related to your niche and it will show results with popular questions and keywords related to your topic. It's an amazing way to get insights into what people are searching online and allows you to identify topics driven by new blog posts or social media content on platforms like Facebook, Instagram, Youtube, and Twitter as well as the types of questions they ask and&nbsp; also want answers.</span><p></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><a href="https://answerthepublic.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Visit&nbsp;Answer The Public From Here</a></span></p>

  <div id="atContainer-05a47ba863f62ec113e14b51b976d14a"></div>
<span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">4. Surfer Seo (SEO Ranking)</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjOUhpQP2O68T9_tM27QAv_umu2RIQxnCSRfjJ9hK0w04j-LEkhxd-7wEhtVKUqTXyCEJZ7agOQFq9A5KBjzwN0g8zyPXwrDMh0RUgUBXjVqKKsSzY_4DleJcS2UA5HeKfev_o7cqESm3Ax0bejSQ48B-889nuJbde7jiVRZ8eTvuf8TrELwgGdjseCZw=s640" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit:-Surfer Seo)</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /><span><br /></span></span></div><p><span><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">With this tool, content creators can quickly and easily check the ranking of their websites and those of other competitors. This tool allows you to see how your website compares to others in different categories, including:&nbsp;</span><p></p><p></p><ul style="text-align: left;"><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Rank Potential</span></li><li><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Organic Search Ranking</span></li></ul><p></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Surfer Seo is free and the interface is very friendly. It's a great tool for anyone who wants to do quick competitor research or check their site's rankings at any time.</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><a href="https://surferseo.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Visit SurferSeo From Here</a></span></p><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">5. Canva (Templates/Graphics)</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjHx5hbdU0ZIHY4IGh8jRKSfmbrXldgc6KgR2KC7qI4Hti-fZmxcJqSB4WsQ9xSMc_lAlvczySNLl1aYHA02zu7wzHrAB81ZggyIApoJt3Y3n7-uDMC4-2xmH7X0kzhuMoGwDGhtpAxbuxbB2fWpWrSPsJ1ybyrJaCMbZHADcWkrfGuVuTJkhEzzvx9qQ=s676" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit:- Canva)</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /><br /></span></div><p><span><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Canva is a free graphic design platform that makes it easy to create invitations, business cards, mobile videos, Instagram posts, Instagram stories, flyers, and more with professionally designed templates. You can even upload your photos and drag and drop them into Canva templates. It's like having a basic version of Photoshop. You can also remove background from images with one click.</span><p></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Canva offers thousands of free, professionally designed templates that can be customized with just a few clicks. Simply upload your photos to Canva, drag them into the template of your choice, and save the file to your computer.</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">It is free to use for basic use but if you want access to different fonts or more features, then you need to buy a premium plan.</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><a href="https://www.canva.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Visit Canva From Here</a></span></p><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">6. Facebook Audience Insights (Audience Research)</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgre3_JAZazKoa9DtY-qK4RXgJKSWBtYWJfbdaNNhmoIpBGFa-n_Ol5ffuL_w6ohklcjWX8zaOnW3PzuB5LnkEsOALNRb1ZyedPDUuqL7zCxJIDmHndfAf3EGkP643w49XMe-QEiDvzvQdPgx0x8Cr7qOTtdNBn9RcH1HdDBll-qEe1dH773lrqW-wNVg=s617" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit:- Facebook Audience Insights</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><p><span><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><span>Facebook Audience Insights is a powerful tool for content creators when researching their target market. This can help you understand the demographics, interests, and behaviors of your target audience. This information helps determine the direction of your content so that it resonates with them. The most important tools to consider in Facebook Audience Insights are Demographics and Behavior. These two sections provide you with valuable information about your target market, such as their age and from where they belong, how much time they spend on social media per day, what devices they use to access it, etc.<br /></span>
<br /></span><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">There is another section of Facebook Audits that is very helpful. This will let you know the interests, hobbies, and activities that people in your target market are most interested in. You can use this information to create content for them about things they will be about as opposed to topics they may not be so keen on.</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><a href="https://www.google.com/search?q=Facebook+Audience+Insights&amp;oq=Facebook+Audience+Insights&amp;aqs=chrome..69i57j69i176j69i58.244j0j4&amp;client=ms-android-transsion-infinix-rev1&amp;sourceid=chrome-mobile&amp;ie=UTF-8" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><span>Visit&nbsp;</span>Facebook Audience Insights From Here</a></span></p><h3 style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">7. Pexels (Images)</span></h3><div><table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEi-CJjqBxkWOZXBVZ7JUGZvxLYWU-icCh0iuL8VWuOoXrCgRuoC59Di9LKh7vCuxm-cCUhQ3FF2nBODoY9vsOX5NgRtKymDp00cXFXYRMc1QyxwMAtsWsmaQiFOAp-d8xZ1VDR3JDaznWbXNSAx2mny3Ti1yM0gngRZta1asKxPK-qB4B7BLCYt0WI1gQ=s1200" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">(Photo Credit: Pixel</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></div><p><span><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">Pexels is a warehouse for any content creator with millions of free royalty images who wants to find high-quality images that can be used freely without having to worry about permissions or licensing so you are free to use the photos in your content and also there is no watermark on photos</span><p></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;">The only cons are that some photos contain people, and Pexels doesn't allow you to remove people from photos. Search your keyword and download as many as you want!</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><a href="https://www.pexels.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Visit Pexel From Here</a></span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></p><p><span style="color: red; font-family: Comfortaa;">So there you have it. We hope that these specially curated websites will come in handy for content creators and small businesses alike. If you've got a site that should be on this list, let us know! And if you're looking for more content creator resources, then let us know in the comments section below</span></p><p><span style="font-family: Comfortaa;"><br /></span></p><p><br /></p>
